        <div class="col-md-2 col-4">
         <div class="blockquote-image">
          <picture>
           <source data-srcset="/media/20911/huntfishr3.png?format=webp&amp;quality=65" type="image/webp">

          </p>
          <p>
           The FWC and its partners are working to increase and diversify participation in hunting and fishing throughout Florida in an effort known as R3 or recruitment, retention, and reactivation. For more information
           <a data-udi="umb://media/3f7ebdb0f37f4844ad8b512c2ad771dc" href="/media/20179/fwfloridasr3plan.pdf" title="Florida's R3 Fishing Action Plan">
            Florida's R3 Fishing Action Plan
           </a>
           and
           <a data-udi="umb://media/2ea0ddee38a3448488534eb9e4dad087" href="/media/20316/r3huntingada.pdf" title="R3huntingADA.pdf">

           </a>
          </p>
